## <a name="supported-operating-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1047">Sistemas operacionais compatíveis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1047">Supported operating systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1048">Há suporte para os seguintes sistemas operacionais:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1048">The following operating systems are supported:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1049">Windows 7 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1049">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1050">Windows Server 2008 R2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1050">Windows Server 2008 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1051">O [servidor HTTP.sys](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (anteriormente chamado de WebListener) não funciona em uma configuração de proxy reverso com o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1051">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1052">Use o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1052">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1053">Para obter mais informações sobre hospedagem no Azure, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1053">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1054">Para obter as diretrizes de solução de problemas, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1054">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1055">Plataformas compatíveis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1055">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1056">Aplicativos publicados para implantação de 32 bits (x86) ou 64 bits (x64) têm suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1056">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1057">Implantar um aplicativo de 32 bits com um SDK do .NET Core de 32 bits (x86), a menos que o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1057">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1058">Exija o maior espaço de endereço de memória virtual disponível para um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1058">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1059">Exija o maior tamanho de pilha do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1059">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1060">Tenha dependências nativas de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1060">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1061">Use um SDK do .NET Core de 64 bits (x64) para publicar um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1061">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1062">Um runtime de 64 bits deve estar presente no sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1062">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1063">O ASP.NET Core vem com o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel), um servidor HTTP padrão multiplataforma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1063">ASP.NET Core ships with [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel), a default, cross-platform HTTP server.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1064">Ao usar o [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) ou o [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview), o aplicativo é executado em um processo separado do processo de trabalho do IIS (*fora do processo*) com o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1064">When using [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) or [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview), the app runs in a process separate from the IIS worker process (*out-of-process*) with the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1065">Como os aplicativos ASP.NET Core são executados em um processo separado do processo de trabalho do IIS, o módulo realiza o gerenciamento de processos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1065">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1066">O módulo inicia o processo para o aplicativo ASP.NET Core quando a primeira solicitação chega e reinicia o aplicativo se ele é desligado ou falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1066">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1067">Isso é basicamente o mesmo comportamento que o dos aplicativos que são executados dentro do processo e são gerenciados pelo [WAS (Serviço de Ativação de Processos do Windows)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1067">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1068">O diagrama a seguir ilustra a relação entre o IIS, o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e um aplicativo hospedado de fora d processo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1068">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![Módulo do ASP.NET Core](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1070">As solicitações chegam da Web para o driver do HTTP.sys no modo kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1070">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1071">O driver roteia as solicitações ao IIS na porta configurada do site, normalmente, a 80 (HTTP) ou a 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1071">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1072">O módulo encaminha as solicitações ao Kestrel em uma porta aleatória do aplicativo, que não seja a porta 80 ou 443.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1072">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app, which isn't port 80 or 443.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1073">O módulo Especifica a porta por meio de uma variável de ambiente na inicialização, e o [middleware de integração do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configura o servidor a ser escutado `http://localhost:{port}` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1073">The module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup, and the [IIS Integration Middleware](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{port}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1074">Outras verificações são executadas e as solicitações que não se originam do módulo são rejeitadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1074">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1075">O módulo não é compatível com encaminhamento de HTTPS, portanto, as solicitações são encaminhadas por HTTP, mesmo se recebidas pelo IIS por HTTPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1075">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding, so requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1076">Depois que o Kestrel coleta a solicitação do módulo, a solicitação é enviada por push ao pipeline do middleware do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1076">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1077">O pipeline do middleware manipula a solicitação e a passa como uma instância de `HttpContext` para a lógica do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1077">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1078">O middleware adicionado pela integração do IIS atualiza o esquema, o IP remoto e pathbase para encaminhar a solicitação para o Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1078">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1079">A resposta do aplicativo é retornada ao IIS, que a retorna por push para o cliente HTTP que iniciou a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1079">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which pushes it back out to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1080">`CreateDefaultBuilder` configura o servidor [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) como o servidor Web e habilita a integração do IIS, configurando o caminho base e a porta para o [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1080">`CreateDefaultBuilder` configures [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) server as the web server and enables IIS Integration by configuring the base path and port for the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1081">O Módulo do ASP.NET Core gera uma porta dinâmica a ser atribuída ao processo de back-end.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1081">The ASP.NET Core Module generates a dynamic port to assign to the backend process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1082">`CreateDefaultBuilder` chama o método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration%2A>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1082">`CreateDefaultBuilder` calls the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration%2A> method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1083">`UseIISIntegration` configura o Kestrel para escutar na porta dinâmica no endereço IP do localhost (`127.0.0.1`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1083">`UseIISIntegration` configures Kestrel to listen on the dynamic port at the localhost IP address (`127.0.0.1`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1084">Se a porta dinâmica for 1234, o Kestrel escutará em `127.0.0.1:1234`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1084">If the dynamic port is 1234, Kestrel listens at `127.0.0.1:1234`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1085">Essa configuração substitui outras configurações de URL fornecidas por:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1085">This configuration replaces other URL configurations provided by:</span></span>

* `UseUrls`
* [<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1086">API de escuta do Kestrel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1086">Kestrel's Listen API</span></span>](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel#endpoint-configuration)
* <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1087">[Configuração](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (ou [opção --urls de linha de comando](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1087">[Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (or [command-line --urls option](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1088">As chamadas a `UseUrls` ou à API `Listen` do Kestrel não são necessárias ao usar o módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1088">Calls to `UseUrls` or Kestrel's `Listen` API aren't required when using the module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1089">Se `UseUrls` ou `Listen` for chamado, o Kestrel escutará na porta especificada somente durante a execução do aplicativo sem o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1089">If `UseUrls` or `Listen` is called, Kestrel listens on the port specified only when running the app without IIS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1090">Para orientação sobre a configuração do Módulo do ASP.NET Core, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1090">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1091">Para saber mais sobre hospedagem, confira [Host no ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1091">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1092">Configuração de aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1092">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1093">Habilitar os componentes de IISIntegration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1093">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1094">Ao criar um host no `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), chame <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder%2A> para habilitar a integração do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1094">When building a host in `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder%2A> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IWebHostBuilder CreateWebHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1095">Para obter mais informações sobre o `CreateDefaultBuilder`, consulte <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1095">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1096">Opções do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1096">IIS options</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1097">Opção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1097">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1098">Padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1098">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1099">Configuração</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1099">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1100">Se `true`, o Servidor do IIS define o `HttpContext.User` autenticado pela [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1100">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1101">Se `false`, o servidor fornecerá apenas uma identidade para `HttpContext.User` e responderá a desafios quando explicitamente solicitado pelo `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1101">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1102">A autenticação do Windows deve estar habilitada no IIS para que o `AutomaticAuthentication` funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1102">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1103">Para obter mais informações, veja [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1103">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1104">Configura o nome de exibição mostrado aos usuários em páginas de logon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1104">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1105">Para configurar opções do IIS, inclua uma configuração de serviço para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1105">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1106">O exemplo a seguir impede que o aplicativo preencha `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1106">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1107">Opção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1107">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1108">Padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1108">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1109">Configuração</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1109">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1110">Se `true`, o [middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) define o `HttpContext.User` autenticado pela [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1110">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1111">Se `false`, o middleware fornecerá apenas uma identidade para `HttpContext.User` e responderá a desafios quando explicitamente solicitado pelo `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1111">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1112">A autenticação do Windows deve estar habilitada no IIS para que o `AutomaticAuthentication` funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1112">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1113">Saiba mais no tópico [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1113">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1114">Configura o nome de exibição mostrado aos usuários em páginas de logon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1114">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1115">Se `true` e o cabeçalho da solicitação `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` estiverem presentes, o `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` será populado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1115">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1116">Servidor proxy e cenários de balanceador de carga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1116">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1117">O [Middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), que configura o Middleware de cabeçalhos encaminhados, e o módulo do ASP.NET Core, são configurados para encaminhar o esquema (HTTP/HTTPS) e o endereço IP remoto de onde a solicitação foi originada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1117">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), which configures Forwarded Headers Middleware, and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the scheme (HTTP/HTTPS) and the remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1118">Configuração adicional pode ser necessária para aplicativos hospedados atrás de servidores proxy adicionais e balanceadores de carga.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1118">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1119">Para obter mais informações, veja [Configurar o ASP.NET Core para trabalhar com servidores proxy e balanceadores de carga](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1119">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1120">Arquivo web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1120">web.config file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1121">O arquivo *web.config* configura o [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1121">The *web.config* file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1122">Criando, transformar e publicar o arquivo *Web.config* é tratado por um destino do MSBuild (`_TransformWebConfig`) quando o projeto é publicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1122">Creating, transforming, and publishing the *web.config* file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1123">Este destino está presente nos destinos do SDK da Web (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1123">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1124">O SDK é definido na parte superior do arquivo de projeto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1124">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1125">Se um arquivo *web.config* não estiver presente no projeto, ele será criado com o *processPath* e os *argumentos* corretos para configurar o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e será transferido para o [resultado publicado](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1125">If a *web.config* file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1126">Se um arquivo *web.config* estiver presente no projeto, ele será transformado com o *processPath* e os *argumentos* corretos para configurar o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e será movido para o resultado publicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1126">If a *web.config* file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1127">A transformação não altera as definições de configuração do IIS no arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1127">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1128">O arquivo *web.config* pode fornecer configurações adicionais do IIS que controlam módulos ativos do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1128">The *web.config* file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1129">Para saber mais sobre os módulos do IIS que podem processar solicitações com aplicativos do ASP.NET Core, veja o tópico [Módulos do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1129">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1130">Para impedir que o SDK da Web transforme o arquivo de *web.config* , use a **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** propriedade no arquivo de projeto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1130">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the *web.config* file, use the **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1131">Ao impedir que o SDK Web transforme o arquivo, o *processPath* e os *argumentos* devem ser definidos manualmente pelo desenvolvedor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1131">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the *processPath* and *arguments* should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1132">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1132">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1133">Local do arquivo web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1133">web.config file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1134">Para configurar o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) corretamente, o arquivo de *web.config* deve estar presente no caminho raiz do [conteúdo](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) (normalmente o caminho base do aplicativo) do aplicativo implantado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1134">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the *web.config* file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1135">Esse é o mesmo local que o caminho físico do site fornecido ao IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1135">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1136">O arquivo *web.config* é necessário na raiz do aplicativo para habilitar a publicação de vários aplicativos usando a Implantação da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1136">The *web.config* file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1137">Existem arquivos confidenciais no caminho físico do aplicativo, como \* \<assembly>.runtimeconfig.jsem*, \* \<assembly> . xml* (comentários de documentação XML) e \* \<assembly>.deps.jsem\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1137">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as *\<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*, *\<assembly>.xml* (XML Documentation comments), and *\<assembly>.deps.json*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1138">Quando o arquivo *web.config* estiver presente e o site for iniciado normalmente, o IIS não atenderá a esses arquivos confidenciais se eles forem solicitados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1138">When the *web.config* file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1139">Se o arquivo *web.config* estiver ausente, nomeado incorretamente ou se não for possível configurar o site para inicialização normal, o IIS poderá servir arquivos confidenciais publicamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1139">If the *web.config* file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1140">**O arquivo de *web.config* deve estar presente na implantação o tempo todo, corretamente nomeado e ser capaz de configurar o site para inicialização normal. Nunca remova o arquivo de *web.config* de uma implantação de produção.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1140">**The *web.config* file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the *web.config* file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1141">Transformação do Web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1141">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1142">Se você precisar transformar o *Web.config* em publicação (por exemplo, definir variáveis ​​de ambiente com base na configuração, no perfil ou no ambiente), consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1142">If you need to transform *web.config* on publish (for example, set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment), see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1143">Configuração do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1143">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1144">**Sistemas operacionais do Windows Server**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1144">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1145">Habilite a função **Servidor Web (IIS)** e estabeleça serviços de função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1145">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1146">Use o assistente **Adicionar Funções e Recursos** por meio do menu **Gerenciar** ou do link no **Gerenciador do Servidor**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1146">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1147">Na etapa **Funções de Servidor**, marque a caixa de **Servidor Web (IIS)**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1147">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)**.</span></span>

   ![A função de Servidor Web IIS é selecionada na etapa Selecionar funções de servidor.](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1149">Após a etapa **Recursos**, a etapa **Serviços de função** é carregada para o servidor Web (IIS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1149">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1150">Selecione os serviços de função do IIS desejados ou aceite os serviços de função padrão fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1150">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![Os serviços de função padrão são selecionados na etapa Selecionar serviços de função.](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1152">**Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1152">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1153">Para habilitar a autenticação do Windows, expanda os seguintes nós: segurança do **servidor Web**  >  **Security**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1153">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1154">Selecione o recurso **Autenticação do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1154">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1155">Para obter mais informações, consulte [autenticação \<windowsAuthentication> do Windows](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurar a autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1155">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1156">**WebSockets (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1156">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1157">O WebSockets é compatível com o ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1157">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1158">Para habilitar WebSockets, expanda os seguintes nós: desenvolvimento de aplicativo de **servidor Web**  >  **Application Development**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1158">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1159">Selecione o recurso **Protocolo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1159">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1160">Para obter mais informações, consulte [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1160">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1161">Continue para a etapa **Confirmação** para instalar os serviços e a função de servidor Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1161">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1162">Uma reinicialização de servidor/IIS não é necessária após a instalação da função do **servidor Web (IIS)** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1162">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1163">**Sistemas operacionais de área de trabalho do Windows**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1163">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1164">Habilite o **Console de Gerenciamento do IIS** e os **Serviços na World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1164">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1165">Navegue até **Painel de Controle** > **Programas** > **Programas e Recursos** > **Ativar ou desativar recursos do Windows** (lado esquerdo da tela).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1165">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1166">Abra o nó **Serviços de Informações da Internet**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1166">Open the **Internet Information Services** node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1167">Abra o nó **Ferramentas de Gerenciamento da Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1167">Open the **Web Management Tools** node.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1168">Marque a caixa de **Console de Gerenciamento do IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1168">Check the box for **IIS Management Console**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1169">Marque a caixa de **Serviços na World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1169">Check the box for **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1170">Aceite os recursos padrão dos **Serviços na World Wide Web** ou personalize os recursos do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1170">Accept the default features for **World Wide Web Services** or customize the IIS features.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1171">**Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1171">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1172">Para habilitar a autenticação do Windows, expanda os seguintes nós: segurança **dos serviços de World Wide Web**  >  **Security**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1172">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1173">Selecione o recurso **Autenticação do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1173">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1174">Para obter mais informações, consulte [autenticação \<windowsAuthentication> do Windows](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurar a autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1174">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1182">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1182">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1183">Instale o *pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core* no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1183">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1184">O pacote instala o tempo de execução do .NET Core, a biblioteca do .NET Core e o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1184">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1185">O módulo permite que aplicativos do ASP.NET Core sejam executados por trás do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1185">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1186">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado antes do IIS, a instalação do pacote deverá ser reparada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1186">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1187">Execute o instalador do pacote de hospedagem novamente depois de instalar o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1187">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1188">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado após a instalação da versão de 64 bits (x64) do .NET Core, os SDKs poderão parecer estar ausentes ([Nenhum SDK do .NET Core foi detectado](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1188">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1189">Para resolver o problema, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1189">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="download"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1190">Baixar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1190">Download</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1191">Navegue até a página [baixar o .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1191">Navigate to the [Download .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1192">Selecione a versão do .NET Core desejada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1192">Select the desired .NET Core version.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1193">Na coluna **Executar aplicativos – runtime**, localize a linha da versão de runtime do .NET Core desejada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1193">In the **Run apps - Runtime** column, find the row of the .NET Core runtime version desired.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1194">Baixe o instalador usando o link **pacote de hospedagem** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1194">Download the installer using the **Hosting Bundle** link.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1195">Alguns instaladores contêm versões de lançamento que atingiram o EOL (fim da vida útil) e não têm mais suporte da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1195">Some installers contain release versions that have reached their end of life (EOL) and are no longer supported by Microsoft.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1196">Para saber mais, confira a [política de suporte](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1196">For more information, see the [support policy](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1197">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1197">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1198">Execute o instalador no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1198">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1199">Os parâmetros a seguir estão disponíveis ao executar o instalador por meio de um shell de comando do administrador:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1199">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1200">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Ignorar a instalação do módulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1200">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1201">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Ignorar a instalação do tempo de execução do .NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1201">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1202">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1202">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1203">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Ignorar a instalação da estrutura compartilhada ASP.NET (ASP.NET Runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1203">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1204">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1204">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1205">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Ignorar a instalação de tempos de execução x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1205">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1206">Use esse parâmetro quando você souber que não hospedará aplicativos de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1206">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1207">Se houver uma possibilidade de hospedar aplicativos de 32 bits e 64 bits no futuro, não use esse parâmetro e instale ambos os runtimes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1207">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1208">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Desabilite a verificação para usar uma configuração compartilhada do IIS quando a configuração compartilhada (*applicationHost.config*) estiver no mesmo computador que a instalação do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1208">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration (*applicationHost.config*) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1209">*Disponível somente para instaladores do ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou Hosting Bundler posterior.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1209">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1210">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1210">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1211">Reinicie o sistema ou execute os seguintes comandos em um shell de comando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1211">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1212">A reinicialização do IIS identifica uma alteração no CAMINHO do sistema, que é uma variável de ambiente, realizada pelo instalador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1212">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1213">Não é necessário interromper manualmente os sites individuais no IIS ao instalar o pacote de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1213">It isn't necessary to manually stop individual sites in IIS when installing the Hosting Bundle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1214">Aplicativos hospedados (sites do IIS) são reiniciados quando o IIS é reiniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1214">Hosted apps (IIS sites) restart when IIS restarts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1215">Os aplicativos são iniciados novamente quando recebem sua primeira solicitação, incluindo a partir do [módulo de inicialização do aplicativo](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1215">Apps start up again when they receive their first request, including from the [Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1216">ASP.NET Core adota o comportamento de roll-forward para versões de patch de pacotes de estrutura compartilhados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1216">ASP.NET Core adopts roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1217">Quando os aplicativos hospedados pelo IIS são reiniciados com o IIS, os aplicativos são carregados com as versões de patch mais recentes de seus pacotes referenciados quando recebem sua primeira solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1217">When apps hosted by IIS restart with IIS, the apps load with the latest patch releases of their referenced packages when they receive their first request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1218">Se o IIS não for reiniciado, os aplicativos serão reiniciados e exibirão o comportamento de roll-forward quando seus processos de trabalho forem reciclados e receberem sua primeira solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1218">If IIS isn't restarted, apps restart and exhibit roll-forward behavior when their worker processes are recycled and they receive their first request.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1219">Para obter informações sobre a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS, consulte [Módulo do ASP.NET Core com a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1219">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1220">Instalar a Implantação da Web durante a publicação com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1220">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1221">Ao implantar aplicativos para servidores com [Implantação da Web](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), instale a versão mais recente da Implantação da Web no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1221">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1222">Para instalar a Implantação da Web, use o [WebPI (Web Platform Installer)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) ou obtenha um instalador diretamente no [Centro de Download da Microsoft](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1222">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1223">O método preferencial é usar o WebPI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1223">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1224">O WebPI oferece uma instalação autônoma e uma configuração para provedores de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1224">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1225">Criar o site do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1225">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1226">No sistema de hospedagem, crie uma pasta para conter arquivos e pastas publicados do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1226">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1227">Em uma etapa a seguir, o caminho da pasta é fornecido ao IIS como o caminho físico para o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1227">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1228">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de arquivo e a pasta de implantação de um aplicativo, confira <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1228">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1229">No Gerenciador do IIS, abra o nó do servidor no painel **conexões** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1229">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1230">Clique com botão direito do mouse na pasta **Sites**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1230">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1231">Selecione **Adicionar Site** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1231">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1232">Forneça um **Nome do site** e defina o **Caminho físico** como a pasta de implantação do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1232">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1233">Forneça a configuração de **Associação** e crie o site selecionando **OK**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1233">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK**:</span></span>

   ![Forneça o Nome do site, o caminho físico e o Nome do host na etapa Adicionar Site.](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1235">Associações de curinga de nível superior (`http://*:80/` e `http://+:80`) **não** devem ser usadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1235">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1236">Associações de curinga de nível superior podem abrir o aplicativo para vulnerabilidades de segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1236">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1237">Isso se aplica a curingas fortes e fracos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1237">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1238">Use nomes de host explícitos em vez de curingas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1238">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1239">Associações de curinga de subdomínio (por exemplo, `*.mysub.com`) não têm esse risco de segurança se você controlar o domínio pai completo (em vez de `*.com`, o qual é vulnerável).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1239">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1240">Veja [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1240">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1241">No nó do servidor, selecione **Pools de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1241">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1242">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do site e selecione **Configurações Básicas** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1242">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1243">Na janela **Editar Pool de Aplicativos**, defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1243">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code**:</span></span>

   ![Defina Sem Código Gerenciado para a versão do CLR do .NET.](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1245">O ASP.NET Core é executado em um processo separado e gerencia o runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1245">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1246">O ASP.NET Core não depende do carregamento do CLR de Área de trabalho (CLR do .NET)&mdash;o Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) para o .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1246">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1247">Definir a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** é opcional, porém recomendado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1247">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1248">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior*: para uma [implantação autocontida](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) de 64 bits (x64) que usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](#in-process-hosting-model), desabilite o pool de aplicativos para processos de 32 bits (x86).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1248">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later*: For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1249">Na barra lateral **Ações** do Gerenciador do IIS > **Pools de Aplicativos**, selecione **Definir Padrões do Pool de Aplicativos** ou **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1249">In the **Actions** sidebar of IIS Manager > **Application Pools**, select **Set Application Pool Defaults** or **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1250">Localize **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits** e defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1250">Locate **Enable 32-Bit Applications** and set the value to `False`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1251">Essa configuração não afeta os aplicativos implantados para a [hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1251">This setting doesn't affect apps deployed for [out-of-process hosting](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1252">Confirme se a identidade do modelo de processo tem as permissões apropriadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1252">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1253">Se a identidade padrão do pool de aplicativos (**modelo de processo**  >  **Identity** ) for alterada **de Identity ApplicationPool** para outra identidade, verifique se a nova identidade tem as permissões necessárias para acessar a pasta, o banco de dados e outros recursos necessários do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1253">If the default identity of the app pool (**Process Model** > **Identity**) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1254">Por exemplo, o pool de aplicativos requer acesso de leitura e gravação às pastas nas quais o aplicativo lê e grava os arquivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1254">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1255">**Configuração de Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1255">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1256">Para saber mais, veja [Configurar a Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1256">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1257">Implantar o aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1257">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1258">Implante o aplicativo na pasta **caminho físico** do IIS que foi estabelecida na seção [Criar o site do IIS](#create-the-iis-site).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1258">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1259">[Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) é o mecanismo recomendado para implantação, mas existem várias opções para mover o aplicativo da pasta *publicar* do projeto para a pasta de implantação do sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1259">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's *publish* folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1260">Implantação da Web com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1260">Web Deploy with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1261">Consulte o tópico [Perfis de publicação do Visual Studio para implantação de aplicativos ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) para saber como criar um perfil de publicação para uso com a Implantação da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1261">See the [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) topic to learn how to create a publish profile for use with Web Deploy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1262">Se o provedor de hospedagem fornecer um Perfil de Publicação ou o suporte para a criação de um, baixe o perfil e importe-o usando a caixa de diálogo **Publicar** do Visual Studio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1262">If the hosting provider provides a Publish Profile or support for creating one, download their profile and import it using the Visual Studio **Publish** dialog:</span></span>

![Página de caixa de diálogo Publicar](index/_static/pub-dialog.png)

### <a name="web-deploy-outside-of-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1264">Implantação da Web fora do Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1264">Web Deploy outside of Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1265">Também é possível usar a [Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) fora do Visual Studio na linha de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1265">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) can also be used outside of Visual Studio from the command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1266">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Ferramenta de Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1266">For more information, see [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span></span>

### <a name="alternatives-to-web-deploy"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1267">Alternativas à Implantação da Web</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1267">Alternatives to Web Deploy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1268">Use qualquer um dos vários métodos para mover o aplicativo para o sistema host, como cópia manual, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) ou [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1268">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="92a07-1270">Procurar no site</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1270">Browse the website</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1271">Depois de implantar o aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem, faça uma solicitação para um dos pontos de extremidade públicos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1271">After the app is deployed to the hosting system, make a request to one of the app's public endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92a07-1272">No exemplo a seguir, o site está associado a um **Nome do Host** IIS de `www.mysite.com` na **Porta** `80`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1272">In the following example, the site is bound to an IIS **Host name** of `www.mysite.com` on **Port** `80`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92a07-1273">É feita uma solicitação para `http://www.mysite.com`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92a07-1273">A request is made to `http://www.mysite.com`:</span></span>
